<div id="review_2712701280" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2712701280" />
    <a title="✨ A ✨ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/65321843-a"><img alt="✨ A ✨ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1604503440p2/65321843.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2712701280?book_show_action=true">Jun 01, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✨ A ✨ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✨ A ✨ " href="/user/show/65321843-a">✨ A ✨ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/28757702-nevernight">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to ✨ A ✨  by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/58818027-fares">Fares</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=read-in-2019">read-in-2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=five-stars">five-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=faves-adult-scifi-and-fantasy">faves-adult-scifi-and-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=all-the-stars-in-the-sky">all-the-stars-in-the-sky</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2712701280" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14746156343151274137"><b>O, my gentlefriends, this book was gLORIOUS.</b><br/>What was I doing before this? I don't remember but my life was sure bleaker before Jay Kristoff blew it to smithereens with this master piece. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Never flinch. Never fear. And never, ever forget.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>Mia Corvere's family was torn apart when she was 10 years old. Her father hung for treason, her mother and baby brother sent to the worst imaginable prison to rot away in the dark. Mia is set on avenging her family but to do that she has to become unstoppabl</span>
  <span id="freeText14746156343151274137" style="display:none"><b>O, my gentlefriends, this book was gLORIOUS.</b><br />What was I doing before this? I don't remember but my life was sure bleaker before Jay Kristoff blew it to smithereens with this master piece. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Never flinch. Never fear. And never, ever forget.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Mia Corvere's family was torn apart when she was 10 years old. Her father hung for treason, her mother and baby brother sent to the worst imaginable prison to rot away in the dark. Mia is set on avenging her family but to do that she has to become unstoppable. So where does one go when one wants to learn how to kill the leader of a country and his lackeys? To the Red Church, school for assassins and servants of the Mother of the Night. <br /><br />This world was so brilliantly developed and thought out. I appreciated that the politics and history was not written in a way that would have bored me to death. Instead I became so invested that I kept notes and was even excited to find out more.<br /><br />I really enjoyed the writing. It is different and you do have to figure things out for yourself. It is not to everyone's taste. The usual YA fantasy of today has made readers used to being spoon fed information so if you're used to that and are not open to using your brain to connect dots then perhaps this book isn't for you ; )<br /><br />The reason I mentioned YA fantasy is because, let's face it, most of the people reading this book are YA readers. <br /><br />Even though the main characters of this book are pretty young (16 y/o) Jay Kristoff is adamant about the fact that these books are not YA. Yes there was plenty sexual content but if you cut that out as well as all the more violent scenes, it did feel YA-ish to me. <br /><br />I really enjoyed figuring things out. It's the reason fantasy is a beloved genre of mine. There were little hints here and there and connecting the dots was so fun and mind-blowing at the same time. <br /><br />I know that many people did not enjoy the footnotes and found them irritating and irrelevant. I thought they were great, filled with witty responses and anecdotes, filled with information that made this world so real to me. <br /><br />These characters, although probably not the best morally, became so dear to me. I was on edge wanting to know what happens next to Mia, what trials she'd have to deal with. <br /><br />This book was such a pleasure and I am so excited to continue this series. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“And just as we mark our places in the pages, those pages leave their marks on us. I can see it in you, sure as I see it in me. You’re a daughter of words. A girl with a story to tell.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />Thanks to my buddy <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/58818027" rel="nofollow noopener">Fares</a> for recommending this book for reading it with me : P<br /><br />______<br />Well well <b>Mr Kristoff, let's see what you've got.</b><br /><blockquote>Buddy reading with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/58818027" rel="nofollow noopener">he who does not appreciate the magnificence of Will Herondale</a>.</blockquote><br /><br />________<br /><b>My reviews for:</b><br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2712704041" rel="nofollow noopener">Godsgrave</a><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2712703982" rel="nofollow noopener">Darkdawn</a><br />  </span>
  <a data-text-id="14746156343151274137" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1528959653" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1528959653" />
    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1528959653?book_show_action=true">Jan 28, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=assassins">assassins</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=2017-reads">2017-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1528959653" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6188041903601347492"><b><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26114463.Nevernight__The_Nevernight_Chronicle___1_' title='Nevernight (The Nevernight Chronicle, #1) by Jay Kristoff' rel='nofollow noopener'>Nevernight</a>, gentlefriends, is an O, so bloody piece of Art.</b><br/><br/>It is not for the faint-hearted. It is not a Young Adult book. It does not feature noble heroes, polished by their acts of kindness. <br/>It is a story of <blockquote>
  <b> killers</b>
</blockquote> <br/>A tale of the vicious fight between <b> <blockquote> Light and Darkness</blockquote></b><br/>And in the shadows cast by the Lady of Blessed Murder, her faithful servants thrive.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506764485i/24050188._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><a href='https://www.redbubble.com/people/phantomrin/collections/591354-nevernight' rel='nofollow noopener'>Source</a><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>“You'll be a rumour. A whisper. The thought that wakes the bastards of this world sweating in the nevernight. The last thing you</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText6188041903601347492" style="display:none"><b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26114463.Nevernight__The_Nevernight_Chronicle___1_" title="Nevernight (The Nevernight Chronicle, #1) by Jay Kristoff" rel="nofollow noopener">Nevernight</a>, gentlefriends, is an O, so bloody piece of Art.</b><br><br>It is not for the faint-hearted. It is not a Young Adult book. It does not feature noble heroes, polished by their acts of kindness. <br>It is a story of <blockquote>
  <b> killers</b>
</blockquote> <br>A tale of the vicious fight between <b> <blockquote> Light and Darkness</blockquote></b><br>And in the shadows cast by the Lady of Blessed Murder, her faithful servants thrive.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506764485i/24050188._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><a href="https://www.redbubble.com/people/phantomrin/collections/591354-nevernight" rel="nofollow noopener">Source</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“You'll be a rumour. A whisper. The thought that wakes the bastards of this world sweating in the nevernight. The last thing you will ever be in this world, girl, is someone's hero.<br>But you will be a girl heroes fear.” </b>
</blockquote><br>In the beautiful and terrible city of Godsgrave, inspired by <b>medieval Venice</b>, a city of Bridges and Bones, where the sky is illuminated by three suns and the God of Light is worshipped, the last daughter of a disgraced <i>familia</i> fled for her life. Swearing revenge. She headed to the finest school of assassins, devoted to the Mother of Darkness. Trained in the fine Arts of Blade. Poison. Seduction. She sang the Song of Death, bathed in Blood, called the Shadows that bowed to her will. But revenge has a steep price. It demands sacrifice. Your conscience. Your soul. And Mia Corvere, the Pale Daughter, the Crow, was tested time after time, only to discover that she was not made of glass. <br>She was steel.<br><blockquote>
  <b>“Never Flinch.<br>Never Fear.<br>And never, ever Forget.” </b>
</blockquote><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26114463.Nevernight__The_Nevernight_Chronicle___1_" title="Nevernight (The Nevernight Chronicle, #1) by Jay Kristoff" rel="nofollow noopener">Nevernight</a>, gentlefriends, is a <b>gritty saga</b>. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4735144.Jay_Kristoff" title="Jay Kristoff" rel="nofollow noopener">Jay Kristoff</a> is not one to shy away from <b>brutality</b>, nor he sugarcoats the actions and the motives of his characters. As the narrator kindly informs us, he does not spare the reader from the gore and the vulgarity. Torture scenes, death, sex scenes, they're all depicted in explicit detail, and while you'll probably want to close your eyes and forget the violence you just witnessed, you can't. But mind that this is not necessarily a bad thing, gentlefriends. Because <b>the ugly and the raw is infused with rare moments of beauty, and humanity</b>. Because the narration is <b>ingenious</b> and <b>witty</b>, and the information regarding the lavish world-building (and other random facts) is presented in the form of footnotes, commented by the mysterious, all-knowing narrator that will make you crack a smile. The prose is unique, elegant, the sarcasm entwined with lyricism, and you can't help but<br><i>read<br>read<br>read</i><br>as if enchanted by a powerful being*.<br><blockquote>
  <b>“When all is bood, blood is all.”</b>
</blockquote><br>While you walk in the filthy streets of Godsgrave, or the dim-lit corridors of the Red Church (the caste of assassins blessed by the All-Mighty Mother), you will meet dubious characters. You will be swept away by politics and murder, and you will try to find a ray of sunshine in acolytes seeking blood, only to be answered with Darkness. Mia Corvere will make you cringe, and curse, and O, this is unexpected, but love. Her courage,her badassery and determination will win you over, and so will her cunning and devious mind. You will follow her wide-eyed in her journey paved with bodies, in the moments she is overwhelmed with lust (for human flesh or for blood), you will participate in the trials she struggles to dominate, and share her heartbreak. Her feeble friendships and longing, and wishes that are not fulfilled. Her nightmares and her questions about who she is. <i>What</i> she is. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506770961i/24051214._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="https://www.redbubble.com/people/phantomrin/collections/591354-nevernight" rel="nofollow noopener">Source</a><br><br>The death toll will take you by surprise. The plot-twists will make you gasp for breath. You will want to hurt <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4735144.Jay_Kristoff" title="Jay Kristoff" rel="nofollow noopener">Jay Kristoff</a>, gentlefriends, the way he hurt you with a seething passion. But if you yearn for a <b>dark tale featuring assassins, smut, ancient magic and a dream of revenge</b>, Mister Kristoff awaits to serve you the <b>delicious and grim story of Mia Corvere</b>.<br><br>*Imperio!<br><br><b>
  <i>You can find, gentlefriends, <a href="http://booknest.eu/reviews/8-kat-reviews/835-nevernight" rel="nofollow noopener">this review</a> and more on <a href="http://booknest.eu/" rel="nofollow noopener">BookNest</a>!</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="6188041903601347492" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('U1DfzEH6TRAuXLKgSz7uEFU51KC4rLfxN5J0y9PuRTSUb4J1OeNQVXNhwm8LmRZjuDe0sY2NKwNm+S1ksfFYrA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('KmrWGi/2Sa0d1TvvRN17nNzzuTRqKg2FRsq254H2RzftVYujV+9U6EDoSyAEeoPvMf3ZJV8LkXcXoe9I4+larw==')})
  }
